ESFM v0.5 JER

Note: This is still a very early look into the unfinished text of the Open English Translation of the Bible. Please double-check the text in advance before using in public. Some things (like capitalisation of ‘him’ referring to Jesus or ‘father’ referring to God) in the RV haven’t been decided yet so we’re still testing both ways.

Note: The Readers’ Version on the left is a translation into contemporary English aimed at the person on the street who hasn’t necessarily been brought up with exposure to Biblical jargon and/or 500-year old English. It’s designed to be used alongside the Literal Version on the right which gives the English reader a window into what’s actually written in the original languages. (See the introduction for more details—we recommend that you read the introduction first if you’re wanting to fully understand the Literal Version.) By comparing the left and right columns, you should be able to easily get the message of the text, while at the same time keeping an eye on what it was actually translated from.

Note that greyed words in the RV are words that the translators consider were most probably in the mind of the writer, but as none of us can double-check with the original speakers or writers, the reader is free to disagree. They are clearly marked because we’ve tried to be as honest and transparent as possible.

The lighter coloured words in the LV are words which aren’t needed in the grammar of the original languages but are required or implied in English. You can read the Key to learn more about them. The underlines in the LV show when one original language word needs to be translated into two or more English words. (Just hide them with the button if you don’t need that information and find it distracting.) Also, the majority of sentences in the LV don’t have the words put into a sensible English order yet. (This should be completed by the end of 2023.)

Jeremiah

It is our prayer that the Open English Translation of the Bible will give you a clear understanding of the accounts and messages written by the God-inspired Biblical writers.

Introduction

Si prupita Hirimiyas, started of work rin isip prupita of 627 leg‑un of not yet born the Messiah and migpabulus until years 580 of not yet born the Messiah. Te malayat timpu of pegpamakey of Hirimiyas, impanpanayan din the people concerning the karereetan egginguma of nasud tenged of sins dan, and of pegsimba ran of me false gods. Ne nakita of Hirimiyas the katumanan of intagne din of timpu nasakup e the Jerusalem of Nibukadnisar King of Babilunya. Nakita rin again the pegkahuhus of siyudad and temple, and the pegkarakep of masulug people duma of King dan there to Babilunya. Intagne din again the return of people puun of pegkarakep dan, and the pegbalew-balew of pegpasasindeg of nasud there to tapey natahuan here.

The Baseen of Hirimiyas nabaad of lalimma: 1.) The calling ki Hirimiyas; 2.) the inlalag of God for of nasud of Huda and of teachers here at time of peghari of Husiyas, Huwakim, Hihuyakin and of Sidikiyas; 3.) the langun nabaybayaan of people sumale of it’s written of Baruk sikritari of Hirimiyas, lagkes the various me pegpanagne, and the important neyitabu of umul of Hirimiyas; 4.) the inlalag of Master God concerning the various lapu there nations; and 5.) the duma pad story concerning the pegkahuhus of Jerusalem, and of pegkaddakep of people peendiye of Babilunya.

Hiid‑uwen person si Hirimiyas; very rin geyinawei the people din, and igkeepes din the eggukum kandan. Due me part of document very the love rin of pegpangguhud concerning the me peg-antus din tenged su in-umew sikandin of God so that egkeyimu prupita. Iling of hapuy there to pusung din the lalag of Master God, and not din iya this igkeeles.

Nasulat again of this document egginguma the timpu duen e new kasabutan. Ne the sika kasabutan eg-ay-ayaran of people of God and egtumanen dan, minsan pad ware teacher egpasuman-suman kandan su igsulat man e this there to me pusung dan. (31:31-34)

Main components of this “book”

The calling ki Hirimiyas 1:1-19

The me pegpanagne concerning the peghari of Husiyas, Huwakim, Huwakin, and of Sidikiyas 2:1-25:38

The nabaybayaan of Hirimiyas 26:1-45:5

The me pegpanagne for of nations 46:1-51:64

The pegkahuhus of Jerusalem 52:1-34

See also the FAQs and the Glossary.
